3.3.2 Labels or Instructions (4 avvik)2 kritisk2 alvorlig
Testregel 3.3.2 (3.3.2 - Nivå A)
CRITICAL

Form input (text) has no accessible label

<input class="searchinput" name="find" placeholder="Søk..." type="text" value=""/>
Add aelement with 'for' attribute, or use aria-label
Testregel 3.3.2 (3.3.2 - Nivå A)
SERIOUS

Input uses placeholder as only label

<input class="searchinput" name="find" placeholder="Søk..." type="text" value=""/>
Add a visibleelement - placeholders disappear when typing

1.3.5 Identify Input Purpose (1 avvik)1 mindre
Testregel 1.3.5 (1.3.5 - Nivå AA)
MINOR

Input appears to be for 'search' but lacks autocomplete

Add appropriate autocomplete attribute for search fields

SVG is missing accessible name

3.3.2 Labels or Instructions (4 avvik)2 kritisk2 alvorlig
Testregel 3.3.2 (3.3.2 - Nivå A)
CRITICAL

Form input (text) has no accessible label

<input class="searchinput" name="find" placeholder="Søk..." type="text" value=""/>
Add aelement with 'for' attribute, or use aria-label
Testregel 3.3.2 (3.3.2 - Nivå A)
SERIOUS

Input uses placeholder as only label

<input class="searchinput" name="find" placeholder="Søk..." type="text" value=""/>
Add a visibleelement - placeholders disappear when typing
Testregel 3.3.2 (3.3.2 - Nivå A)
CRITICAL

Form input (text) has no accessible label

<input class="searchinput" name="find" placeholder="Hva kan vi hjelpe deg med?" type="text" value=""/>
Add aelement with 'for' attribute, or use aria-label
Testregel 3.3.2 (3.3.2 - Nivå A)
SERIOUS

Input uses placeholder as only label

<input class="searchinput" name="find" placeholder="Hva kan vi hjelpe deg med?" type="text" value=""/>

1.3.5 Identify Input Purpose (1 avvik)1 mindre
Testregel 1.3.5 (1.3.5 - Nivå AA)
MINOR

Input appears to be for 'search' but lacks autocomplete

<input class="searchinput" name="find" placeholder="Søk..." type="text" value=""/>
Add appropriate autocomplete attribute for search fields
